        if (
          args.length > 3 &&
          args[2] === 2 &&
          typeof args[3] === 'boolean'
        ) {
          gdprApplies = args[3];
          if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
            args[2]('set', true);
          }
        }
      } else if (args[0] === 'ping') {
        var retr = {
          gdprApplies: gdprApplies,
          cmpLoaded: false,
          cmpStatus: 'stub'
        };

        if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
          args[2](retr);
        }
      } else {
        queue.push(args);
      }
    }

    function postMessageEventHandler(event) {
      var msgIsString = typeof event.data === 'string';
      var json = {};

      try {
        if (msgIsString) {
          json = JSON.parse(event.data);
        } else {
          json = event.data;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      var payload = json.__tcfapiCall;

      if (payload) {
        window.__tcfapi(
          payload.command,
          payload.version,
          function(retValue, success) {
            var returnMsg = {
              __tcfapiReturn: {
                returnValue: retValue,
                success: success,
                callId: payload.callId
              }
            };
            if (msgIsString) {
              returnMsg = JSON.stringify(returnMsg);
            }
            event.source.postMessage(returnMsg, '*');
          },
          payload.parameter
        );
      }
    }

    while (win) {
      try {
        if (win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]) {
          cmpFrame = win;
          break;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      if (win === window.top) {
        break;
      }
      win = win.parent;
    }
    if (!cmpFrame) {
      addFrame();
      win.__tcfapi = tcfAPIHandler;
      win.addEventListener('message', postMessageEventHandler, false);
    }
  };

  makeStub();

  var uspStubFunction = function() {
    var arg = arguments;
    if (typeof window.__uspapi !== uspStubFunction) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        if (typeof window.__uspapi !== 'undefined') {
          window.__uspapi.apply(window.__uspapi, arg);
        }
      }, 500);
    }
  };

  var checkIfUspIsReady = function() {
    uspTries++;
    if (window.__uspapi === uspStubFunction && uspTries < uspTriesLimit) {
      console.warn('USP is not accessible');
    } else {
      clearInterval(uspInterval);
    }
  };

  if (typeof window.__uspapi === 'undefined') {
    window.__uspapi = uspStubFunction;
    var uspInterval = setInterval(checkIfUspIsReady, 6000);
  }
})();

             <amp-img alt="‘Huge success’ as half of UK adults receive Covid-19 vaccine – Matt Hancock" height="9px" layout="responsive" src="https://cdn.jwplayer.com/v2/media/qo3AdTjD/poster.jpg?width=720" width="16px">

            <div class="videoDetail">
             <h2 class="">
              ‘Huge success’ as half of UK adults receive Covid-19 vaccine – Matt Hancock
             </h2>

          <script type="text/javascript">
           var event = new Event("playIncVideoSetupReady");document.dispatchEvent(event);
              
              const containerId = "video-section-playinc-component";
              var script = document.createElement('script');
              script.defer = 'true';
              script.src = 'https://cdn.jwplayer.com/libraries/EmFwauGg.js';
              document.head.appendChild(script);

              let current_mediaid, adTag;
    
              const enrichTag = (adTag, mediaid, adUnit, gs_channels, topictags, gdpr, gdprConsent, addtlConsent, permutiveSegments) => {
                let customParams = '';
                customParams += 'videoID=' + mediaid;
                customParams += '&gs_channels=' + gs_channels;
                customParams += '&topictags=' + topictags;
                
                if(permutiveSegments){
                    customParams += '&permutive=' + permutiveSegments;
                }
                const tagUrl = new URL(adTag);
                const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(tagUrl.search);
                const encodedCustomParams = encodeURIComponent(customParams);
                if (urlParams.has('cust_params')) {
                    if (urlParams.get('cust_params') !== '') {
                        adTag = adTag.replace(/(cust_params[^&]+)/, '$1' + '%26' + encodedCustomParams);
                    } else {
                        adTag = adTag.replace(/(cust_params[^&]+)/, '$1' + encodedCustomParams);
                    }
                } else {
                    adTag = adTag + '&cust_params=' + encodedCustomParams;
                }
                adTag += '&gdpr=' + gdpr;
                adTag += '&gdpr_consent=' + gdprConsent;
                adTag += '&addtl_consent=' + addtlConsent;
                if (adUnit && adUnit !== 'null') {
                  adTag = adTag.replace(/(iu=).*?(&)/,'$1' + adUnit + '$2',);
                }
                return adTag;
              };

              const replaceVideoID = (adTag, mediaid) => {
                  console.log('using',mediaid);
                  return adTag.replace(/(videoID%3D).*?(%26)/, '$1' + mediaid + '$2');
              };

              const updateAdTag = (mediaid) => {
                if (jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag) {
                    adTag = jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag;
                    adTag = replaceVideoID(adTag, mediaid);
                    jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag = adTag;
                } else {
                    adTag = jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule[0].tag;
                    adTag = replaceVideoID(adTag, mediaid);
                    jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule[0].tag = adTag;
                }
                console.log('section adTag:', adTag);
              };

              const playIncVideoSetup = (args) => {
                const { 
                  videoAdUnitPath, 
                  gs_channels,
                  topictags,
                  gdpr,
                  gdprConsent,
                  addtlConsent,
                  permutiveSegments,
                } = args;

                jwplayer(containerId).setup({
                    playlist: 'https://cdn.jwplayer.com/v2/media/3PBPrpGY',
                    autoPause: {
                        viewability: true,
                        pauseAds: true,
                    },
                });

                jwplayer(containerId).on('ready', function () {
                    current_mediaid = jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().playlistItem.mediaid;
                    if (jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag) {
                        adTag = jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag;
                        adTag = enrichTag(
                            adTag, 
                            current_mediaid, 
                            videoAdUnitPath, 
                            gs_channels,
                            topictags,
                            gdpr,
                            gdprConsent,
                            addtlConsent,
                            permutiveSegments
                        );
                        jwplayer(containerId).getConfig().advertising.schedule[0].tag = adTag;
                    } else {
                        adTag = jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule[0].tag;
                        adTag = enrichTag(
                            adTag, 
                            current_mediaid, 
                            videoAdUnitPath, 
                            gs_channels,
                            topictags,
                            gdpr,
                            gdprConsent,
                            addtlConsent,
                            permutiveSegments
                        );
                        jwplayer.defaults.advertising.schedule[0].tag = adTag;
                    }
                    console.log('section adTag:', adTag);
                });
              };

              const iframe = document.querySelector('.videohub-section .heroHolder iframe');
              const heading = document.querySelector('.videohub-section .heroHolder h2');
              const videos = document.querySelectorAll('.videohub-section .otherVideosHolder .videoHolder');
              const isPlayingClass = "isPlaying";

              const switchVideo = (video) => {
                return (e) =>  {
                  if(!video.classList.contains(isPlayingClass)){
                    jwplayer(containerId).load('https://cdn.jwplayer.com/v2/media/' + video.dataset.mediaid);
                    updateAdTag(video.dataset.mediaid);
                    jwplayer(containerId).play();
                    heading.textContent = video.dataset.title;
                    videos.forEach((video) => {
                      video.classList.remove(isPlayingClass);
                    });
                    video.classList.add(isPlayingClass);
                  }
                }
              }

              videos.forEach((video) => {
                video.addEventListener("click", switchVideo(video));
              });
          </script>
         </div>
